| <input type="checkbox"/> |3000|Maximum Area of Longest Diagonal Rectangle|45.80%|Easy|[link](https://leetcode.com/problems/maximum-area-of-longest-diagonal-rectangle?envType=problem-list-v2&envId=nethpi8g)|

<script>
// Key for storing checkbox states in localStorage
const STORAGE_KEY = 'checkbox_states';

// Function to save checkbox state to localStorage by index
function saveCheckboxState(checkbox, index) {
    const states = getStoredStates();
    states[index] = checkbox.checked;
    localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(states));
}

// Function to get stored states from localStorage
function getStoredStates() {
    const stored = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY);
    return stored ? JSON.parse(stored) : {};
}

// Function to restore checkbox states from localStorage
function restoreCheckboxStates() {
    const states = getStoredStates();
    const checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]');

    checkboxes.forEach((checkbox, index) => {
        if (states.hasOwnProperty(index.toString())) {
            checkbox.checked = states[index.toString()];
        }
    });
}

// Function to add event listeners to all checkboxes
function initializeCheckboxPersistence() {
    const checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]');

    checkboxes.forEach((checkbox, index) => {
        checkbox.addEventListener('change', function() {
            saveCheckboxState(this, index);
        });
    });
}

function colorDifficultyCells() {
    // Get all table cells (td and th elements)
    const cells = document.querySelectorAll('td, th');

    cells.forEach(cell => {
        const cellText = cell.textContent.trim().toLowerCase();

        // Check for difficulty levels and apply colors
        if (cellText === 'easy') {
            cell.style.color = '#28a745'; // Green
        } else if (cellText === 'medium') {
            cell.style.color = '#ffc107'; // Yellow
        } else if (cellText === 'hard') {
            cell.style.color = '#dc3545'; // Red
        }
    });
}

function colorAcceptanceCells() {
  const table = document.querySelector('table');
  if (!table) return;

  const rows = table.querySelectorAll('tr');

  rows.forEach(row => {
    const cells = row.querySelectorAll('td');

    // Assuming the percentage is in a specific column, e.g., the last one
    const percentageCell = cells[3];

    if (percentageCell && percentageCell.textContent.includes('%')) {
      const percentageText = percentageCell.textContent.replace('%', '').trim();
      const percentage = parseFloat(percentageText);
      console.log(percentage);

      if (!isNaN(percentage)) {
        if (percentage >= 70) {
          percentageCell.style.color = '#28a745';
        } else if (percentage >= 40) {
          percentageCell.style.color = '#ffc107';
        } else {
          percentageCell.style.color = '#dc3545';
        }
      }
    }
  });
};

// Initialize when DOM is loaded
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    // First restore the states from previous session
    restoreCheckboxStates();
    // Then add event listeners to save state on each toggle
    initializeCheckboxPersistence();

    document.querySelector('.md-button').addEventListener('click', clearCheckboxStates);

    colorDifficultyCells();

    colorAcceptanceCells();
});

// Optional: Function to clear all stored checkbox states
function clearCheckboxStates() {
    localStorage.removeItem(STORAGE_KEY);
    // Optionally uncheck all checkboxes
    const checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]');
    checkboxes.forEach(checkbox => {
        checkbox.checked = false;
    });
}
</script>
